Context: <ModMetaData><name>Hazbin Hotel Outfits</name><author>Shenix</author><supportedVersions><li>1.2</li><li>1.3</li><li>1.4</li><li>1.5</li></supportedVersions><url>Link</url><packageId>Shenix.HazbinHotel</packageId><picture>thumbnail.png</picture><description>

    Adds some outfits from Hazbin Hotel.
	
	
This mod adds most of the current Main Character cast of Hazbin Hotel as apparel and hairstyles to RimWorld.
If you want to make your own happy Hell hotel in the game :D
	
This mod can be added in later playthroughs, and should not have conflicts with other mods (as far as I know).
	
	Current Characters include:
-Charlie
-Vaggie
-Alastor
-Angel Dust
-Husker (Both with and without wings versions)
-Nifty

I might add even more characters to this mod later!


Keep in mind that because the textures are made by myself, I didn't include different sizes for different outfits, as I'd rather just focus on adding more characters instead of tweaking the same outfit for different bodytypes.
So certain character outfits will only show up on a specific body type, and be "invisible" on the rest (though they will still get the stats and everything as if they are wearing it).
For example Charlie will only work on the Average Female model, and Angel's Outfit will only work on thin, etc.

I don't have much modding experience, so expect some bugs and mistakes. Be sure to let me know.

Character designs are from Hazbin Hotel and Amazon. 
Textures by me (Shenix).
